<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Le malade imaginaire
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">The Imaginary Invalid
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Charpentier,_Marc-Antoine" title="Category:Charpentier, Marc-Antoine">Charpentier, Marc-Antoine</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>H.495
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IMC 122
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Moli%C3%A8re" title="Category:Molière">Molière</a> (1622-1673)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>French
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices</i>: haut-dessus, dessus, haute-contre, taille, basse + mixed chorus (SSATB)<br /><i>Orchestra</i>: strings + continuo
</td></tr></table>
</div>
